Here is the annotated script in the exact format and structure shown in the example:


<Scene Heading>FADE IN:</Scene Heading>

<NARRATIVE>A PAIR OF SMOKESTACKS AGAINST AN ORANGE AUTUMN SUN SKY...</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>TOMBSTONES blend into a NEVER-ENDING SEA OF MIDDLE-CLASS ROW HOUSES in the distance, and nothing seems to separate the two.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>A NEWLY DUG GRAVE is in the LOWER LEFT-HAND CORNER of our FRAME.</NARRATIVE>

<NARRATIVE>MILITARY DRUMS. HUNDREDS of POLICEMEN, in their DRESS BLUES, ENTER from FRAME RIGHT. A FEW COPS CARRY a COFFIN.</NARRATIVE>
